
-----title

id='poem_sentence_1_254255'>数<span class='inlineComment2'>（赵本作几）</span>声离岸橹，几<span class='inlineComment2'>（赵本作数）</span>点别州山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_254255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_254255'>野客犹思住，江鸥亦忘还。<div id='poem_sentence_2_254255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_254255'>隔墙歌舞地，喧静不相关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_253965'>王业致艰难，功成退自安。<div id='poem_sentence_0_253965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_253965'>闲中犹有俸，品外更无官。<div target='_blank'>赠孙何状元</a><span class='authorDate'>（992年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34390, "北宋", "魏野", id='poem_sentence_0_254256'>天非道莫尊，道非贤莫存。<div id='poem_sentence_0_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_254256'>始知贤人生，与道为轮辕<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_254256'>明庭亲选士，虑彼贤愚浑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_254256'>天子至文明，擢公为状元。<div id='poem_sentence_3_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_254256'>一榜三百人，默默谁复言。<div id='poem_sentence_4_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_254256'>有如凤在林，众鸟不敢喧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_254256'>威棱廌有角，度量海无垠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_254256'>直入仲尼室，不顾孟轲门。<div id='poem_sentence_7_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_254256'>文得古中新，陈熟甚已<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作矣）</span>冤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_254256'>一字如一星，光芒不见痕。<div id='poem_sentence_9_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_254256'>首官来理陕，棠树换枯根。<div id='poem_sentence_10_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_254256'>淑气春风和，美化冬日暄。<div id='poem_sentence_11_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_254256'>至诚物莫欺，至明物莫昏。<div id='poem_sentence_12_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_254256'>平思治地陕，清欲变河源。<div id='poem_sentence_13_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_254256'>我生三十年，未尝离丘园。<div id='poem_sentence_14_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_254256'>朴性昧巧习，惟知道可敦。<div id='poem_sentence_15_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_254256'>贫巷无富车，闲地唯云屯。<div id='poem_sentence_16_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_254256'>我愿为松竹，生在君子轩。<div id='poem_sentence_17_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_254256'>早夜接清风，节高阴更繁。<div id='poem_sentence_18_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_254256'>何当亲教授，如渴饮衢樽。<div id='poem_sentence_19_254256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_254256'>斯言拙且直，堪将鬼神论。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年</a>　约于本年秋，居乡，有诗送杨甫。作品：同大孙状元送杨甫之蒲中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《钜鹿东观集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_253975' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_253975_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_253975'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_253975'>蒲本舜都州，君思独去游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_253975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_253975'>云分五老顶<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作岭）</span>，河喷二妃楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_253975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_253975'>雨足禾初<span class='inlineComment2'>（旧山楼本作果全）</span>熟，霜迟叶尚稠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_254214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_254214'>琴怜徽外声弥澹，酒爱篘中味更醇。<div id='poem_sentence_10_254214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_254002'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_254002'>长安君到转民安，夏少炎蒸腊少寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_254002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_254002'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_254002_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>约于本年，居乡，有诗谢孙仅寄蜀笺及茶。作品：谢长安孙舍人寄惠蜀笺并茶二首。<span id='poem_sentence_1_254178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_254178'>旋烧陆羽烹茶鼎，忙换陶潜漉酒巾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_254178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_254178'>可爱水边松竹上，数朝犹自有香尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_254178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_254178'></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_254177'>平生未竖降旗客，临老将为弃甲人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_254177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_254177'>豸角勇无心害物，鸡皮怯有汗沾巾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_253982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_253982'>贳酒村穿红树过，读书寺入翠岚游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_253982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_253982_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1018&endYear=1018')">1018年</a>　本年，居乡，有诗寄薛奎。作品：寄淮南制置使薛户部。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《钜鹿东观集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_254241' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_254241' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/254241?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_4_254241'>数道转输归检察，满朝才子动吟誇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_254241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_254241'>搜寻奸诈穷毫发，举荐廉<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_31_254244'>古人何卑屑，束缚于名迹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_31_254244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_254244'></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_254244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_254244'><span class='label'>按：</span>以上《钜鹿东观集》卷一○<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_254244_0'>⑴ 原作碧，据旧山楼本、张本、章本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_254244_0'>⑵ 旧山楼本、张本、四库本作遇</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_254244_0'>⑶ 用晦（二字原缺，据章本、张本补，赵本作识）</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_254244_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年8月30日</a>　八月三十日，与僧用晦等游中条山，联句赋诗。作品：解城条山。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《钜鹿东观集》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_254254' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_254254' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/254254?labeling=true' target='_blank'>解城条山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（994年8月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34390, "北宋", "魏野", "poem_title_254254")'>魏野</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_254254_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_254254_0'>① 并序（原无题，据旧山楼本、章本、温校补）</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_254254'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_254254'>万仞云根泉，清泠濯我足<span class='inlineComment2'>（用晦）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_254254'>森森沧<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>爪甲，凛凛寒肌肉<span class='inlineComment2'>（衢）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_254254'>来初自试探，坐久频舒缩<span class='inlineComment2'>（野）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_254254'>触开浪花白，踏破苔衣绿<span class='inlineComment2'>（衢）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_254254'>肺腑亦清泠，形影相照烛<span class='inlineComment2'>（用晦）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_254254'>忽罢避游鱼，未归妨渴鹿<span class='inlineComment2'>（野）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_254254'>惧浊远泥沙，就阴怜草木<span class='inlineComment2'>（衢）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_254254'>浸润易调畅，狎玩难羁束<span class='inlineComment2'>（识）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_254254'>欲伐我未能，先起人何速<span class='inlineComment2'>（野）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_254254'>此会高且闲，愿继渔父躅<span class='inlineComment2'>（用晦）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_254254'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_254254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_254254'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_254254_0'>⑴ 旧山楼本、张本、四库本作洒，赵本、章本作露</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_254254_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4492c79dfc824129bb3fc33721a6c61e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4492c79dfc824129bb3fc33721a6c61e");'><span id='4492c79dfc824129bb3fc33721a6c61e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>，45岁</div><div id='4492c79dfc824129bb3fc33721a6c61e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　约于本年，在西京留台李建中筵席上分韵赋诗。作品：陪留台李学士筵上赋得文石酒杯分得杯字。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《钜鹿东观集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_254123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_254123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/254123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪留台李学士筵上赋得文石酒杯分得杯字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34390, "北宋", "魏野", "poem_title_254123")'>魏野</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_254123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_254123'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_254123'>知自何山得，磨砻作酒杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_254123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_254123'>斟疑五色动，醉认一拳开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_254123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_254123'>洼似泉舂出，痕如藓渍来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_254123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_254123'>主人心朴素，爱惜过璚瑰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_254123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_254123'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_254123_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
河津
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ca48c35f277a4b339e43283ccc39cd79_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ca48c35f277a4b339e43283ccc39cd79");'><span id='ca48c35f277a4b339e43283ccc39cd79_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年</a>，53岁</div><div id='ca48c35f277a4b339e43283ccc39cd79' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年</a>　约于本年，登龙门县楼，有诗。作品：登龙门县楼与知宰刘大著将话别因有题纪。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《钜鹿东观集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_254157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_254157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/254157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登龙门县楼与知宰刘大著将话别因有题纪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1012年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34390, "北宋", "魏野", "poem_title_254157")'>魏野</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_254157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_254157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_254157'>名士为官处，登楼景好题。<div id='poem_sentence_0_254157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_254157'>县城蚕市闹，村墅<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作野）</span>鹊巢低。<div id='poem_sentence_1_254157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_254157'>日暖园蔬嫩，烟晴垄麦齐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_254157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_254157'>长宜同此望，那忍话分携。<div id='poem_sentence_3_254157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_254157'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_254157_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
